â”‚ CRITICAL BUG #3 FOUND in RegisterView: Line 36 of diff shows confirmPassword isValidTest does `v === form.fields.password.value`. This creates a closure over form.fields.password.value AT DEFINITION TIME. Since form is being constructed, this captures the initial ref, but the isValidTest function is NOT reactive. When password changes, confirmPassword validation won't re-evaluate against new password value unless explicitly re-validated. This breaks the "passwords must match" validation!   â”‚

â”‚ Cross-reference: RegisterView's signUp() calls form.validate() before submission (line 103 in diff). useFormValidation.validate() (line 153-157) calls validate() on each field, which WILL execute isValidTest with current password value. So AT SUBMIT TIME, validation catches mismatched passwords. BUT it's a UX bug - between typing and submitting, UI could show green borders when passwords don't match. User sees green, thinks it's valid, but submit fails. Severity: MEDIUM (not data corruption, but poor UX).   â”‚
